### A

<p><b>abandon </b><span class="sign">[ə'bændən]</span> v./n.放弃；放纵</p>
<p><b>abase </b><span class="sign">[ə'beis]</span> v. 降低自己，贬抑，使卑下</p>
<p><b>abash </b><span class="sign">[ə'bæʃ]</span> v.使害羞，使尴尬</p>
<p><b>abate </b><span class="sign">[ə'beit]</span> v.减轻，减少</p>
<p><b>abbreviate </b><span class="sign">[ə'bri:vieit]</span> v.缩短；缩写</p>
<p><b>abdicate </b><span class="sign">['æbdikeit]</span> v.退位，辞职，放弃</p>
<p><b>abduct </b><span class="sign">[æb'dʌkt]</span> v. 绑架，拐走</p>
<p><b>aberrant </b><span class="sign">[æ'berənt]</span> a.越轨的；异常的</p>
<p><b>aberration </b><span class="sign">[,æbə'reiʃən]</span> n.离开正路，脱离常轨；变形</p>
<p><b>abet </b><span class="sign">[ə'bet]</span> v.教唆，鼓励，帮助</p>
<p><b>abeyance </b><span class="sign">[ə'beiəns]</span> n.中止，搁置</p>
<p><b>abhor </b><span class="sign">[əb'hɔ:]</span> v.憎恨，嫌恶</p>
<p><b>abhorrent </b><span class="sign">[əb'hɔrənt]</span> a.可恨的，讨厌的</p>
<p><b>abide </b><span class="sign">[ə'baid]</span> v.容忍，忍受</p>
<p><b>abject </b><span class="sign">['æbdʒekt]</span> a.极可怜的;卑下的</p>
<p><b>abjure </b><span class="sign">[əb'dʒuə]</span> v.发誓放弃</p>
<p><b>ablution </b><span class="sign">[ə'blu:ʃən]</span> n.(宗教的)净礼，沐浴</p>
<p><b>abnegate </b><span class="sign">['æbniɡeit]</span> v.否认，放弃</p>
<p><b>abnegation </b><span class="sign">[,æbni'ɡeiʃən]</span> n. 放弃; 自我牺牲</p>
<p><b>abolish </b><span class="sign">[ə'bɔliʃ]</span> v.废止，废除(法律、制度、习俗等)</p>
<p><b>abolition </b><span class="sign">[æbə'liʃən]</span> n.废除，革除</p>
<p><b>abominate </b><span class="sign">[ə'bɔmineit]</span> v.痛恨；厌恶</p>
<p><b>aboriginal </b><span class="sign">[,æbə'ridʒənəl]</span> n. 原始居民，土著</p>
<p><b>abortive </b><span class="sign">[ə'bɔ:tiv]</span> a. 无结果的，失败的</p>
<p><b>abound </b><span class="sign">[ə'baund]</span> v. 充满; 富于</p>
<p><b>aboveboard </b><span class="sign">[ə'bʌv,bɔ:d]</span> a./adv.光明正大的(地)</p>
<p><b>abrade </b><span class="sign">[ə'breid]</span> v.磨损，磨小</p>
<p><b>abrasion </b><span class="sign">[ə'breiʒən]</span> n.表面磨损</p>
<p><b>abrasive </b><span class="sign">[ə'breisiv]</span> a.磨损的；生硬粗暴的</p>
<p><b>abreast </b><span class="sign">[ə'brest]</span> adv.并列，并排</p>
<p><b>abridge </b><span class="sign">[ə'bridʒ]</span> v.删减；缩短</p>
<p><b>abrogate </b><span class="sign">['æbrəuɡeit]</span> v.废止，废除</p>
<p><b>abrupt </b><span class="sign">[ə'brʌpt]</span> a突然的，意外的；唐突的</p>
<p><b>abscission </b><span class="sign">[æb'siʒən] n.[医]切除，截去；[植]</span>脱离</p>
<p><b>abscond </b><span class="sign">[əb'skɔnd]</span> v.潜逃，逃亡</p>
<p><b>absenteeism </b><span class="sign">[æbsən'ti:iz(ə)m]</span> n.旷课，旷工</p>
<p><b>absolute </b><span class="sign">['æbsəlu:t]</span> a.绝对的，完全的; 无(条件)限制的</p>
<p><b>absolve </b><span class="sign">[əb'zɔlv]</span> v.赦免，免除</p>
<p><b>absorb </b><span class="sign">[əb'sɔ:b]</span> v.吸收；同化；吸引„的注意</p>
<p><b>abstain </b><span class="sign">[əb'stein]</span> v.禁绝，放弃</p>
<p><b>abstemious </b><span class="sign">[æb'sti:mjəs]</span> a.有节制的，节俭的(eating & drinking)</p>
<p><b>abstention </b><span class="sign">[æb'stenʃən]</span> n.节制</p>
<p><b>abstentious </b><span class="sign">[əb'stenʃəs]</span> a.节制的</p>
<p><b>abstinent </b><span class="sign">['æbstinənt]</span> a. 饮食有度的，有节制的，禁欲的</p>
<p><b>abstract </b><span class="sign">['æbstrækt]</span> n.摘要；a.抽象的</p>
<p><b>abstruse </b><span class="sign">[æb'stru:s]</span> a.难懂的，深奥的</p>
<p><b>absurd </b><span class="sign">[əb'sə:d]</span> a.荒谬的，可笑的</p>
<p><b>abundance </b><span class="sign">[ə'bʌndəns]</span> n.充裕，多量</p>
<p><b>abundant </b><span class="sign">[ə'bʌndənt]</span> a.丰富的，盛产的</p>
<p><b>abuse </b><span class="sign">[ə'bju:z]</span> v./n.辱骂; 滥用</p>
<p><b>abusive </b><span class="sign">[ə'bju:siv]</span> a.漫骂的；毁谤的；虐待的</p>
<p><b>abut </b><span class="sign">[ə'bʌt]</span> v.接界，毗连</p>
<p><b>abysmal </b><span class="sign">[ə'bizməl]</span> a.极深的；糟透的</p>
<p><b>academic </b><span class="sign">[,ækə'demik]</span> a.学院的，学术的；理论的</p>
<p><b>academician </b><span class="sign">[ə,kædə'miʃən]</span> n.院士；学会会员</p>
<p><b>acarpous </b><span class="sign">[ei'kɑ:pəs]</span> a. 不结果实的</p>
<p><b>accede </b><span class="sign">[æk'si:d]</span> v.同意</p>
<p><b>accelerate </b><span class="sign">[æk'seləreit]</span> v.加速；促进</p>
<p><b>accentuate </b><span class="sign">[æk'sentjueit]</span> v.重读；强调</p>
<p><b>access </b><span class="sign">['ækses]</span> n.通路；途径</p>
<p><b>access </b><span class="sign">[access]</span> v. 得到；使用</p>
<p><b>accessible </b><span class="sign">[ək'sesəbl]</span> a.易达到的；易受影响的</p>
<p><b>accessory </b><span class="sign">[æk'sesəri]</span> a.附属的，次要的</p>
<p><b>acclaim </b><span class="sign">[ə'kleim]</span> v.欢呼，称赞</p>
<p><b>acclimate </b><span class="sign">[ə'klaimit]</span> v.使服水土; 使适应</p>
<p><b>accolade </b><span class="sign">['ækəleid]</span> n.推崇；赞扬</p>
<p><b>accommodate </b><span class="sign">[ə'kɔmədeit]</span> v.与„一致；提供食宿</p>
<p><b>accommodating </b><span class="sign">[ə'kɔmədeitiŋ]</span> a.乐于助人的</p>
<p><b>accompany </b><span class="sign">[ə'kʌmpəni]</span> v.伴随，陪伴</p>
<p><b>accomplice </b><span class="sign">[ə'kɔmplis]</span> n.同谋者，帮凶</p>
<p><b>accomplish </b><span class="sign">[ə'kɔmpliʃ]</span> v.完成，做成功</p>
<p><b>accomplished </b><span class="sign">[ə'kɔmpliʃt]</span> a.完成了的；有技巧的，有造诣的</p>
<p><b>accord </b><span class="sign">[ə'kɔ:d]</span> v./n.同意；一致</p>
<p><b>accost </b><span class="sign">[ə'kɔst]</span> v.搭话</p>
<p><b>accountability </b><span class="sign">[ə,kautə'biliti]</span> n.负有责任</p>
<p><b>accrete </b><span class="sign">[æ'kri:t]</span> v.逐渐增长；添加生长；连生</p>
<p><b>accretion </b><span class="sign">[æ'kri:ʃən]</span> n.自然的增加；增加物</p>
<p><b>accrue </b><span class="sign">[ə'kru:]</span> v.(利息等)增大；增多</p>
<p><b>accumulate </b><span class="sign">[ə'kju:mjuleit]</span> v.积聚，积累(collect)</p>
<p><b>accuracy </b><span class="sign">['ækjurəsi]</span> n.精确，准确</p>
<p><b>accurate </b><span class="sign">['ækjurit]</span> a.精确的，准确的</p>
<p><b>accuse </b><span class="sign">[ə'kju:z]</span> v.谴责，指责</p>
<p><b>acerbic </b><span class="sign">[ə'sə:bik]</span> a.苦涩的；刻薄的</p>
<p><b>acerbity </b><span class="sign">[ə'sə:biti]</span> n. 涩，酸，刻薄</p>
<p><b>achromatic </b><span class="sign">[,ækrəu'mætik]</span> a. 非彩色的，无色的</p>
<p><b>acknowledge </b><span class="sign">[ək'nɔlidʒ]</span> v.承认；致谢</p>
<p><b>acme </b><span class="sign">['ækmi]</span> n.顶点，极点</p>
<p><b>acolyte </b><span class="sign">['ækəlait]</span> n.(教士的)助手，侍僧</p>
<p><b>acorn </b><span class="sign">['eikɔ:n]</span> n.橡子，橡果</p>
<p><b>acoustic </b><span class="sign">[ə'ku:stik]</span> a.听觉的，有关声音的</p>
<p><b>acquaint </b><span class="sign">[ə'kweint]</span> v.使„熟知；通知</p>
<p><b>acquaintance </b><span class="sign">[ə'kweintəns]</span> n.熟知；熟人</p>
<p><b>acquainted </b><span class="sign">[ə'kweintid]</span> a.对某事物熟悉的；对某人认识的</p>
<p><b>acquiesce </b><span class="sign">[,ækwi'es]</span> v.勉强同意，默许</p>
<p><b>acquired </b><span class="sign">[ə'kwaiəd]</span> a.后天习得的</p>
<p><b>acquisitive </b><span class="sign">[ə'kwizitiv]</span> a.渴望得到的，贪婪的</p>
<p><b>acquit </b><span class="sign">[ə'kwit]</span> v.宣告无罪；脱卸义务和责任；还清(债务)</p>
<p><b>acquittal </b><span class="sign">[ə'kwit(ə)l]</span> n.宣告无罪，开释</p>
<p><b>acrid </b><span class="sign">['ækrid]</span> a.辛辣的，刻薄的</p>
<p><b>acrimonious </b><span class="sign">[ækri'məunjəs]</span> a.尖刻的，严厉的</p>
<p><b>acrimony </b><span class="sign">['ækriməni]</span> n.尖刻，刻薄</p>
<p><b>acrobat </b><span class="sign">['ækrəbæt]</span> n.特技演员，杂技演员</p>
<p><b>acronym </b><span class="sign">['ækrənim]</span> n. 首字母缩略词</p>
<p><b>acrophobia </b><span class="sign">[,ækrəu'fəubjə]</span> n.恐高症</p>
<p><b>actuarial </b><span class="sign">[,æktju'eəriəl]</span> a. (保险)精算的，保险计算的</p>
<p><b>actuate </b><span class="sign">['æktjueit]</span> v. 驱使，激励</p>
<p><b>acuity </b><span class="sign">[ə'kjuiti]</span> n.(尤指思想或感官)敏锐</p>
<p><b>acumen </b><span class="sign">[ə'kju:mən]</span> n.敏锐，精明,聪明</p>
<p><b>acute </b><span class="sign">[ə'kju:t] a.灵敏的；[病]</span>急性的</p>
<p><b>adage </b><span class="sign">['ædidʒ]</span> n.格言，古训</p>
<p><b>adamant </b><span class="sign">['ædəmənt]</span> a.强硬的；固执的</p>

<p><b>adaptable </b><span class="sign">[ə'dæptəbl]</span> a.有适应能力的；可改编的</p>
<p><b>addendum </b><span class="sign">[ə'dendəm]</span> n.补充，附录</p>
<p><b>addict </b><span class="sign">[ə'dikt]</span> v./n.沉溺；上瘾(者)</p>
<p><b>addition </b><span class="sign">[ə'diʃən]</span> n.增加，附加</p>
<p><b>additive </b><span class="sign">['æditiv]</span> n.添加剂</p>
<p><b>addle </b><span class="sign">['ædl]</span> v. 使腐坏; 使昏乱</p>
<p><b>address </b><span class="sign">[ə'dres]</span> v.处理，对付，着手解决；致词</p>
<p><b>adduce </b><span class="sign">[ə'dju:s]</span> v. 给予(理由); 举出(例证)</p>
<p><b>adept </b><span class="sign">['ædept]</span> a.老练的，精通的</p>

<p><b>adlib </b><span class="sign">[æd'lib]</span> v. 临时讲话，即兴表演</p>

### F

### G

### I

<p><b>icicle </b><span class="sign">['aisikl]</span> n.冰柱，冰垂</p>
<p><b>icing </b><span class="sign">['aisiŋ]</span> n. 糖衣，糖霜</p>
<p><b>icon </b><span class="sign">['aikɔn]</span> n.圣像，偶像</p>
<p><b>iconoclast </b><span class="sign">[ai'kɔnəklæst]</span> n.攻击传统观念或风俗的人</p>
<p><b>iconoclastic </b><span class="sign">[ai,kɔnə'klæstik]</span> a.对传统观念(或惯例)进行攻击的</p>
<p><b>ideology </b><span class="sign">[,aidi'ɔlədʒi]</span> n.思想体系，思想意识，意识形态</p>
<p><b>idiom </b><span class="sign">['idiəm]</span> n.习语，语言的习惯用法；特色</p>
<p><b>idle </b><span class="sign">['aidl]</span> a.(指人)无所事事的；无效的；v.懒散，无所事事</p>
<p><b>idol </b><span class="sign">['aidl]</span> n. 神像；偶像</p>
<p><b>idolater </b><span class="sign">[ai'dɔlətə]</span> n.神像(偶像)崇拜者</p>
<p><b>idolatrize </b><span class="sign">[ai'dɔlətraiz]</span> v. 奉为偶像，盲目崇拜</p>
<p><b>idolize </b><span class="sign">['aidəlaiz]</span> v. 将„当作偶像崇拜；极度喜爱或仰慕</p>
<p><b>idyll </b><span class="sign">['idil]</span> n.田园生活；田园诗</p>
<p><b>igneous </b><span class="sign">['iɡniəs]</span> a.火的，含火的</p>
<p><b>ignite </b><span class="sign">[iɡ'nait]</span> v.发光；点燃，燃烧</p>
<p><b>ignoble </b><span class="sign">[iɡ'nəubl]</span> a.卑鄙的</p>
<p><b>ignominious </b><span class="sign">[iɡnə'miniəs]</span> a.可耻的；耻辱的</p>
<p><b>ignominy </b><span class="sign">['iɡnəmini]</span> n.羞耻，屈辱</p>
<p><b>ignorant </b><span class="sign">['iɡnərənt]</span> a.无知的，愚昧的</p>
<p><b>illegal </b><span class="sign">[i'li:ɡəl]</span> a.违法的</p>
<p><b>illegible </b><span class="sign">[i'ledʒəbl]</span> a. 难读的，难认的</p>
<p><b>illegitimate </b><span class="sign">[,ili'dʒitimit]</span> a.不合法的；私生的</p>
<p><b>illiberal </b><span class="sign">[i'libərəl]</span> a. 气量狭窄的</p>
<p><b>illicit </b><span class="sign">[i'lisit]</span> a.违法的</p>
<p><b>illiterate </b><span class="sign">[i'litərit]</span> a.文盲的</p>
<p><b>illuminate </b><span class="sign">[i'lju:mineit]</span> v.阐明，解释；照亮</p>
<p><b>illuminati </b><span class="sign">[i,lu:mi'nɑ:ti]</span> n.先觉者，智者</p>
<p><b>illusion </b><span class="sign">[i'lu:ʒən]</span> n.假象，错觉</p>
<p><b>illusive </b><span class="sign">[i'lu:siv]</span> a.迷惑人的，迷幻的</p>
<p><b>illusory </b><span class="sign">[i'lu:səri]</span> a.虚幻的</p>
<p><b>illustrate </b><span class="sign">['iləstreit]</span> v.为„作插图或图表；说明，阐明</p>
<p><b>illustrious </b><span class="sign">[i'lʌstriəs]</span> a. 著名的，显赫的</p>
<p><b>imbecile </b><span class="sign">['imbisail]</span> n. 心智能力极低的人</p>

<style type="text/css">
.sign {
    color: #999999;
}

.cont-link {
    padding-right: 10px; 
}

#middle-linkings {
    display: none;
    position: fixed;
    top: 10%;
    right: 10%;
    z-index: 100;
}
</style>

<script type="text/javascript">
    window.onscroll = function () {
        let scrollPos = getScrollTop();
        console.log("scrollPos：",scrollPos);
        if (scrollPos >= 500) {
            var middleLinkings = document.getElementById("middle-linkings");
            middleLinkings.style.display = "block";
            // alert();
        } else {
            var headLinkings = document.getElementById("middle-linkings");
            headLinkings.style.display = "none";
        }
    }
    /**
     * 获取滚动条位置
     */
    function getScrollTop() {
        console.log("moving")
        var scrollPos;
        if (window.pageYOffset)
        {
            scrollPos = window.pageYOffset;
        }
        else if (document.compatMode && document.compatMode != 'BackCompat')
        {
            scrollPos = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
        }
        else if (document.body)
        {
            scrollPos = document.body.scrollTop;
        }
        return scrollPos;
    }
</script>
